<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карманный.html>карма́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">karmánnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pocket
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карманный.html>карма́нное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:издание.html>изда́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>karmánnoje</b> izdánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pocket edition</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карманный.html>карма́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:словарь.html>слова́рь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>karmánnyj</b> slovárʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pocket dictionary</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карманный.html>карма́нные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>karmánnyje</b> časý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pocket watch</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карманный.html>карма́нные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>karmánnyje</b> dénʹgi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pocket money</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карманный.html>карма́нные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:расход.html>расхо́ды</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>karmánnyje</b> rasxódy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">minor expenses</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карманный.html>карма́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>вор</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>karmánnyj</b> vor</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pickpocket</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карманный.html>карма́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кража.html>кра́жа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>karmánnaja</b> kráža</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pickpocketing</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***карниз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:карниз.html>карни́з</a> (8322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Karnies</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карниз.html>карни́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">karníz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карниз.html>карни́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карниз.html>карни́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карниз.html>карни́зов</a></b>)
</p>

***карта.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рта</a> (862)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">karta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рта</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kárta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рт</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>map</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chart</li>
<li>card</li>
<li>playing card</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> menu</li>
<li>patch (of asphalt on a road)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремонт.html>ремо́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорожный.html>доро́жного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:покрытие.html>покры́тия</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́ртами</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">remónt doróžnovo pokrýtija <b>kártami</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">repair of the road surface in patches</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***картавить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картавить.html>карта́вить</a> (28437)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картавить.html>карта́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to burr, to mispronounce some sounds, to especially [r] and, to less commonly [l]</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***картина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a> (621)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">cartina</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fine paper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>picture (representation of visible reality produced by drawing, etc.)</li>
<li>painting, canvas</li>
<li>movie, film</li>
<li>picture, image (as produced in transient fashion by technology, e.g. a monitor)</li>
<li>scene</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>For sense 1, this term is often used in the sense of referring to a painting created by hand and perceived as a work of art. On the other hand, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нка</a></i> is preferably used for photographs and other non-transient images created with the help of technology.
</p>

***картинка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нка</a> (2926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartínka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: a small picture, photograph or illustration; icon</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This term is typically used in a general fashion to refer to images, photographs etc., with a tendency of usage for creations that were made with the help of technology. In terms of refering to drawings, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a></i> is mainly used for hand-made paintings and often carries a sense of referring to a perceived work of art.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картинно.html>карти́нно</a> (17749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинный.html>карти́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartínnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинно.html>карти́нно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartínno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-карти́нно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)карти́ннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-карти́нно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)карти́нней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>expressively</li>
<li>picturesquely, in a picturesque manner, with external beauty</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинный.html>карти́нный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kartínnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">карти́нность</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kartínnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинный.html>карти́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartínnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)карти́ннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)карти́нней</b>)

***картон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картон.html>карто́н</a> (12393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">carton</i> or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Karton</i>, both borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">cartone</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картон.html>карто́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картон.html>карто́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картон.html>карто́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картон.html>карто́нов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картонный.html>карто́нный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cardboard, paperboard</li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Айсман позвонил в специальную <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">картотеку</span> и попросил техническую запись допроса пастора Шлага штандартенфюрером Штирлицем 29 сентября 1944 года. <span title="<a href = vnd.unilang:пропуск.html>про́пуск</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одного́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́скольких</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цитируемый.html>цити́руемом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:текст.html>те́ксте</a>" style="cursor: help">❬…❭</span> ― Что, записей не осталось? ― Нет, ― ответили ему из <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">картотеки</span>, ― записи в интересах операции не велись… </span></li>
</ul></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ка́рточ(ка)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kártoč(ka)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карточный.html>ка́рточный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kártočnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> card
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карточный.html>ка́рточный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:домик.html>до́мик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kártočnyj</b> dómik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">house of cards</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карточный.html>ка́рточная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kártočnaja</b> sistéma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rationing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картошка.html>карто́шка</a> (2014)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">карто́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartóxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a dialectal form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картофель.html>карто́фель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartófelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Recorded since the middle of the 19th century. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">карто́(фель)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartó(felʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-шка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картошка.html>карто́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartóška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картошка.html>карто́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картошка.html>карто́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картошка.html>карто́шек</a></b>)

***карцер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:карцер.html>ка́рцер</a> (10203)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carcer</i> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Karzer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карцер.html>ка́рцер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kárcer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карцер.html>ка́рцера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карцер.html>ка́рцеры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карцер.html>ка́рцеров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lockup; punishment cell; sweatbox, isolation ward</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:карьерный.html>карье́рный</a> (29398)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карьера.html>карье́ра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">karʹjéra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карьерный.html>карье́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">karʹjérnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> career</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карьера.html>карье́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">karʹjér</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карьерный.html>карье́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">karʹjérnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> full gallop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карьерный.html>карье́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:аллюр.html>аллю́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>karʹjérnyj</b> alljúr</i> ― <span class="e-translation">full-gallop pace</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> open-pit mine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:карьерный.html>карье́рные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>karʹjérnyje</b> rabóčije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">open-pit mine workers</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***касаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:касаться.html>каса́ться</a> (991)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">касатисѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kasatisę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kasati</i> + reflexive <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sę</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:касаться.html>каса́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kasátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коснуться.html>косну́ться</a></b>) (+ genitive case)
</p>
<ol><li>to touch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:касаться.html>каса́емся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кончик.html>ко́нчиком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языка́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:верхний.html>ве́рхней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губы́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kasájemsja</b> kónčikom jazyká vérxnej gubý.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We touch the upper lip with the tip of the tongue. (from "<a href = vnd.unilang:малыш.html>Малыш</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>у́чится</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a> - The baby is learning to speak" by Anna Gerasimova)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to concern, to have to do with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:касаться.html>каса́ется</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto tebjá ne <b>kasájetsja</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This doesn't concern you.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">touch</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трогать.html>тро́гать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">trógatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дотрагиваться.html>дотра́гиваться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dotrágivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
